        height: 100%;
        margin: 8px auto
      }

      .djlz .desktopSparkle__asinsContainer--oneAsin > .desktopSparkle__asinContainer, .djlz .desktopSparkle__asinsContainer--twoAsins > .desktopSparkle__asinContainer {
        max-width: none
      }

      .djlz .desktopSparkle__asinsContainer--oneAsin > .desktopSparkle__asinContainer {
        width: 100%
      }

      .djlz .desktopSparkle__asinsContainer--twoAsins > .desktopSparkle__asinContainer {
        width: calc((100% - 10px) / 2)
      }

        -ms-overflow-x: visible
